THIRD-PARTY SOFTWARE NOTICES

This file lists the third-party open-source components distributed with
rocm-cli, together with their versions and the full text of their licenses.
The components are grouped by license; each license text appears once and lists
every component it covers. This file is generated from the project's dependency
lockfile by `cargo xtask tpn`; do not edit it by hand.
